***bedlam.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bedlam.html>bedlam</a> (47804)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i><a href = vnd.unilang:bedlam.html>Bedlam</a>,</i> alternative name of the English lunatic asylum, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bethlem_Royal_Hospital" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Bethlem Royal Hospital">Bethlem Royal Hospital</a></i> (royal hospital from 1375, mental hospital from 1403) (earlier <i>St <a href = vnd.unilang:mary.html>Mary</a> of Bethlehem outside Bishopsgate,</i> hospice in existence from 1329, priory established 1247), since used to mean “a place or situation of madness and chaos”. <i><a href = vnd.unilang:bedlam.html>Bedlam</a></i> as name of hospital attested 1450.
</p><p>Phonologically, corruption of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">Bethlem</i>, itself a corruption of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">Bethlehem</i> (the Biblical town), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">Βηθλεέμ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Bēthleém</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Biblical_Hebrew" class="extiw" title="w:Biblical Hebrew">Biblical Hebrew</a></span> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="he">בֵּית לֶחֶם</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="he-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bêṯ leḥem</span>, literally <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">house of bread</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bedlam.html>bedlam</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">bedlams</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A place or situation of chaotic uproar, and where confusion prevails.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1888</b>,  H.H. Giles,  <cite>The The Insane, and the Wisconsin System for their Care</cite>, page 18:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Some of the <a href = vnd.unilang:wards.html>wards</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> veritable "<b>bedlams</b>," and discharged patients have <a href = vnd.unilang:told.html>told</a> of <i>abuses</i> practiced in them of which the <a href = vnd.unilang:meren.html>mere</a> recital causes a shudder.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2002</b>,  Mark L. Friedman,  <cite>Everyday Crisis Management</cite>, page 134:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">The outside of the Hyatt <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bedlam.html>bedlam</a></b>. There <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> a group of more than a hundred injured people on the circular drive in front of the <a href = vnd.unilang:hotel.html>hotel</a>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2005</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kazuo_Ishiguro" class="extiw" title="w:Kazuo Ishiguro">Kazuo Ishiguro</a>,  <cite>Never Let <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>Me</a> Go</cite>, page 31:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">A car <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> a rarity, and the sight of one in the distance <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> sometimes enough to cause <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bedlam.html>bedlam</a></b> during a class.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2020</b> June 3,  <a href = vnd.unilang:sam.html>Sam</a> Mullins OBE discusses with Stefanie Foster,  “LTM: a new chapter begins at 40”, in  <cite>Rail</cite>, page 54:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">"<a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> an extraordinary February <a href = vnd.unilang:half.html>half</a> term <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> I think <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> 22,000 visitors in the seven days. Which actually <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a bit like <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bedlam.html>bedlam</a></b> at times."</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An insane person; a lunatic; a madman.
<ul><li><b>ca. 1605</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>, <i>King Lear</i>, Act III, sc. 7:
<dl><dd>Let's follow the old <a href = vnd.unilang:earl.html>Earl</a>, and get the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bedlam.html>Bedlam</a></b></dd>
<dd>To lead him where he would; his roguish madness</dd>
<dd>Allows itself to anything.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1678</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Bunyan" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:John Bunyan">John Bunyan</a>, <i>The Pilgrim's Progress</i>, Christian overtakes Faithful:
<dl><dd>The <a href = vnd.unilang:pilgrims.html>pilgrims</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> clothed with such <a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a> of raiment as <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> diverse from the raiment of any that traded in that fair. The people, therefore, of the fair, made a great gazing upon them: some <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> they <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> fools, some they <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> <b>bedlams</b>, and some they are outlandish <a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>men</a>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A lunatic asylum; a madhouse.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1720</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Archbishop_Tillotson" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Archbishop Tillotson">Archbishop Tillotson</a>,  <cite>The works of the Most Reverend <a href = vnd.unilang:dr.html>Dr</a>. John Tillotson</cite>, page 43:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">But if any <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a> should profess to believe these <a href = vnd.unilang:things.html>things</a>, and yet allow himself in any known wickedness, such a one should be put into <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bedlam.html>bedlam</a></b>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><b>1824</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lord_Byron" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Lord Byron">Lord Byron</a>, <i>Don Juan</i>, Canto XIV:lxxxiv:
<dl><dd>Shut up the world at large, let <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bedlam.html>Bedlam</a></b> out;</dd>
<dd>And you will be perhaps surprised to find</dd>
<dd>All <a href = vnd.unilang:things.html>things</a> pursue exactly the same route,</dd>
<dd>As now with those of <i>soi-disant</i> sound mind.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1843</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Charles_Dickens" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Charles Dickens">Charles Dickens</a>, "A Christmas <a href = vnd.unilang:carol.html>Carol</a>":
<dl><dd>“There’s another fellow,” muttered Scrooge; who overheard him: “my clerk, with fifteen <a href = vnd.unilang:shillings.html>shillings</a> a week, and a wife and family, talking about a merry Christmas. I’<a href = vnd.unilang:ll.html>ll</a> retire to <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bedlam.html>Bedlam</a></b>.”</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>ca. 1909</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mark_Twain" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Mark Twain">Mark Twain</a>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:letters.html>Letters</a> from the Earth</i>, Letter II:
<dl><dd>... only the holy can stand the joys of that <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bedlam.html>bedlam</a></b>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
</body> 
***bedlegerig.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bedlegerig.html>bedlegerig</a> (52402)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">bedleger</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bedrest</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ig</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-y, -ish</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

</p>

<li><span class="use-with-mention">  imperative of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bedoelen.html>bedoelen</a></i></span></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***bedotten.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bedotten.html>bedotten</a> (19712)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>A merger of two earlier verbs:
</p>
<ul><li><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">bedodden</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">deceive</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">dodden</i>.</li>
<li><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bedotten.html>bedotten</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">confuse</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">dotten</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:dutten.html>dutten</a></i>.</li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bedotten.html>bedotten</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to mislead, to trick</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to cheat, to scam</li></ol>

***bedpan.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bedpan.html>bedpan</a> (71060)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bed.html>bed</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">pan</i> ("chamber <a href = vnd.unilang:pot.html>pot</a>").
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bedpan.html>bedpan</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">bedpans</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A pan used for urination and defecation while in <a href = vnd.unilang:bed.html>bed</a>, now usually for reasons of medical necessity or convenience.
<dl><dd><i> The nurse emptied the patient's <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bedpan.html>bedpan</a></b> each morning. </i></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bedrieglijk.html>bedrieglijk</a> (28328)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bedriegelijc</i>. </p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bedrieglijk.html>bedrieglijk</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bedrieglijk.html>bedrieglijker</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">bedrieglijkst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>deceitful (<i><a href = vnd.unilang:regarding.html>regarding</a> one's character</i>)</li>
<li>fraudulent (<i><a href = vnd.unilang:regarding.html>regarding</a> one's practices</i>)</li>
<li>deceptive (<i><a href = vnd.unilang:regarding.html>regarding</a> one's <a href = vnd.unilang:looks.html>looks</a></i>)</li>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:bedrijf.html>bedrijf</a></i>. Equivalent to a deverbal from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bedrijven.html>bedrijven</a></i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Betrieb</i>.

***bedrink.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bedrink.html>bedrink</a> (95447)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">*bedrinken</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">bedrincan</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to <a href = vnd.unilang:drink.html>drink</a> in, <a href = vnd.unilang:drink.html>drink</a> up, absorb</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; conflated with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">bidrenchen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to soak up, steep</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">bedrencan</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to drench completely</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">be-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:drink.html>drink</a></i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">be-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">drench</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">bedrinken</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to <a href = vnd.unilang:drink.html>drink</a> up, get drunk</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">betrinken</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to get drunk</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bedrink.html>bedrink</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">bedrinks</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">bedrinking</b>, <i>simple past</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past-form-of" lang="en">bedrank</b>, <i>past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">bedrunk</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">bedrunken</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive, intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To <a href = vnd.unilang:drink.html>drink</a> in; <a href = vnd.unilang:drink.html>drink</a> up; <a href = vnd.unilang:drink.html>drink</a> to the fullest
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1860</b>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:walter.html>Walter</a> Thornbury,  <cite>Turkish life and character</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">[...] not far from Tophana — the place of cannons — and doth there foolishly, selfishly, and sottishly <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bedrink.html>bedrink</a></b> himself unroyally drunk with bottle after bottle of <a href = vnd.unilang:champagne.html>champagne</a>, [...]</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1889</b>,  Solomon <a href = vnd.unilang:caesar.html>Caesar</a> Malan,  <cite>Original notes on the Book of Proverbs</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">"Thus the unsteady woman [<b>bedrinks</b>] intoxicates the firm and <a href = vnd.unilang:resolute.html>resolute</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a>."</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">reflexive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to get drunk
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1899</b>,  University of Virginia,  <cite>The Virginia spectator</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">That "moreover it behooveth to scourge all such heretics as would have it that these herein-afore-mentioned swineherds <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> <b>bedrunk</b> themselves and <a href = vnd.unilang:did.html>did</a> cunningly adduce this tale of witchery to the end that they might escape meet [...]"</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:bedwelmen.html>bedwelmen</a></i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">be-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">dwelme</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wooziness, fool</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">-en</i>. No exact cognates are found, but related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">fordwielman</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gothic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gothic language">Gothic</a></span> <i class="Goth mention" lang="got">𐌳𐍅𐌰𐌻𐌼𐍉𐌽</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="got-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dwalmōn</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:bedwingen.html>bedwingen</a></i>. ***beek.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:beek.html>beek</a> (10337)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bēke</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">beki</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*bakiz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***beeldhouwen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:beeldhouwen.html>beeldhouwen</a> (42574)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Backformation from <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beeldhouwer.html>beeldhouwer</a></span> ("scuptor"); in turn from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beeld.html>beeld</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:houwen.html>houwen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beeldhouwen.html>beeldhouwen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to carve (sculptures, as an art form)</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>The verb <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a backformation from a noun "<i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beeldhouwer.html>beeldhouwer</a></i>" meaning "sculptor", which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> why it follows a weak verb inflection pattern as opposed to class 7 strong verb pattern that the base verb, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:houwen.html>houwen</a></i> (<i><a href = vnd.unilang:houwen.html>hieuw</a></i>/<i><a href = vnd.unilang:gehouwen.html>gehouwen</a></i>), <a href = vnd.unilang:belongs.html>belongs</a> to.
</p>

<p><a href = vnd.unilang:gerund.html>Gerund</a> of the verb <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beeldhouwen.html>beeldhouwen</a></i>.
</p>

***been.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> (1275)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bêen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">bēn</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*bainą</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:benen.html>benen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beentje.html>beentje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:leg.html>leg</a>, limb of a person, horse (other animals' would have <i><a href = vnd.unilang:poten.html>poten</a></i>) and certain <a href = vnd.unilang:objects.html>objects</a> (again many have <i><a href = vnd.unilang:poten.html>poten</a></i>)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:benen.html>benen</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:passer.html>passer</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The <a href = vnd.unilang:legs.html>legs</a> of a pair of compasses.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mathematics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> side, <a href = vnd.unilang:leg.html>leg</a>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:benen.html>benen</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoek.html>hoek</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The sides of an angle.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes_2">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li>The contemporary plural <i><a href = vnd.unilang:benen.html>benen</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> derived from an analogy to other nouns with regular plurals. Originally, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> left unchanged in the plural; such use in preserved only in set phrases like <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">upright, standing, awake</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beenderen.html>beenderen</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:benen.html>benen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beentje.html>beentje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>bone, constituent part of a skeleton.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> bone, the chalky material <a href = vnd.unilang:bones.html>bones</a> are made of</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bēre</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*bero</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*berô</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beer.html>beer</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beren.html>beren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beertje.html>beertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>bear, any member of the family Ursidae
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:beer.html>beer</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:drinkt.html>drinkt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bier.html>bier</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The <b>bear</b> drinks <a href = vnd.unilang:beer.html>beer</a>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> person who <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> physically impressive and/or crude
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>Wat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:beer.html>beer</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vent.html>vent</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:daar.html>daar</a> voorin, he?</i>
<dl><dd><i>What a <b>bear</b> of a guy there in front, <a href = vnd.unilang:huh.html>huh</a>?</i></dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>

<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:122px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/43/Buttress_on_Bunge_church%2C_2009-08-11.jpg/120px-Buttress_on_Bunge_church%2C_2009-08-11.jpg" decoding="async" width="120" height="179" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/43/Buttress_on_Bunge_church%2C_2009-08-11.jpg/180px-Buttress_on_Bunge_church%2C_2009-08-11.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/43/Buttress_on_Bunge_church%2C_2009-08-11.jpg/240px-Buttress_on_Bunge_church%2C_2009-08-11.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2592" data-file-height="3872" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:beer.html>beer</a></i> of <i>steunbeer</i>. — A <i>buttress</i>.</div></div></div>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bêer</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*bēr</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*bairaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_6">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beer.html>beer</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beren.html>beren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beertje.html>beertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>boar (male swine)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kinderboerderij.html>kinderboerderij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heeft.html>heeft</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aantal.html>aantal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zeugen.html>zeugen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> één <b><a href = vnd.unilang:beer.html>beer</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The petting zoo <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> a number of sows and only one <b>boar</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>buttress; protective external construction, notably against ice or supporting the weight of the main building</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beer.html>beer</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beren.html>beren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beertje.html>beertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">now dialectal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> liquid manure <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">excrement gathered in a pit to fertilize</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wie.html>Wie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:doet.html>doet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nu.html>nu</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:beer.html>beer</a></b> in <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bier.html>bier</a>? <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:haat.html>haat</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:beer.html>beer</a></b>!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Who in the world would put <b>liquid manure</b> in his <a href = vnd.unilang:beer.html>beer</a>? I hate <b>manure</b>!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Bär</i>. Cognate to etymology 1.
</p>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beer.html>beer</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beren.html>beren</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">college <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> debt
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>Door</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gokverslaving.html>gokverslaving</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zat.html>zat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:enorme.html>enorme</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:beer.html>beer</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:opgescheept.html>opgescheept</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Due to her gambling addiction she <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> saddled with an enormous <b>debt</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schuld.html>schuld</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>

***beest.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:beest.html>beest</a> (1299)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">beeste</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:beste.html>beste</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:beste.html>beste</a></i>, like <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">beast</i> (which see for more).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beest.html>beest</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beesten.html>beesten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beestje.html>beestje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>An animal, a beast.
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>Er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zit.html>zit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:beestje.html>beestje</a></b> in m'n <a href = vnd.unilang:soep.html>soep</a>.</i>
<dl><dd>There <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a <b>bug</b> in my soup.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li>An animal kept as livestock, a head.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A cruel, wild, uncivilised, uninhibited or brutal person.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> folteraars <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> grenspolitie <a href = vnd.unilang:waren.html>waren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sadistische.html>sadistische</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:beesten.html>beesten</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The torturers of the border police <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> sadistic <b>beasts</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>Ze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:beest.html>beest</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">She's a <b>beast</b> in <a href = vnd.unilang:bed.html>bed</a>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:beest.html>Beest</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> a somewhat negative (or at least savage) connotation, whereas <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dier.html>dier</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> neutral.</li>
<li>In compounds, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:beest.html>beest</a></i> can have the meaning “someone who enjoys an activity”; compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">animal</i> in <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">party animal</i> and also <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">beast</i>.</li></ul>

***beet.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:beet.html>beet</a> (2974)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bēte</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*biti</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*bitiz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beet.html>beet</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beten.html>beten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beetje.html>beetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>bite</li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:bete.html>bete</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">bēta</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:beffen.html>beffe</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cap, collar</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">biffe</i>. Further origin uncertain. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Beffchen</i>.

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bef.html>bef</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beffen.html>beffen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:befje.html>befje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> collar</li>
<li>an ornamental pair of <a href = vnd.unilang:bands.html>bands</a> worn hanging <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> the chest, notably as part of formal dress by magistrates, <a href = vnd.unilang:professors.html>professors</a> and certain Catholic and Protestant clergy</li>
<li>by analogy, any of certain other similar <a href = vnd.unilang:objects.html>objects</a></li>
<li>a patch on the throat or chest of a different color on <a href = vnd.unilang:cats.html>cats</a> or dogs</li>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:begaan.html>begaan</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to walk upon, to tread on
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vanaf.html>Vanaf</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:morgen.html>morgen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kunnen.html>kunnen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:steigers.html>steigers</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:begaan.html>begaan</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">They will be able to <b>walk on</b> the <a href = vnd.unilang:piers.html>piers</a> from tomorrow on.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> by extension</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to move upon, to travel on
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wegen.html>wegen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hier.html>hier</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:erg.html>erg</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moeilijk.html>moeilijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:begaan.html>begaan</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The roads <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> here are very difficult to <b>travel upon</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to commit (e.g. a <a href = vnd.unilang:misdeed.html>misdeed</a>)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wie.html>Wie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jullie.html>jullie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heeft.html>heeft</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:deze.html>deze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moord.html>moord</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:begaan.html>begaan</a></b>?</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Which one of you <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <b>committed</b> this murder?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> mostly with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:laten.html>laten</a></i></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to do, to act as one wills</li></ol>
